 1322 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     88 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/03F4               | *   6-5  Sound fading, 0 = normal, 1 = low, 2 = medium, 3 = high
 1323 |  3   nda_lacie_routines.s     89 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/03F4               | *   4-1  Undetermined, apparently always zero
